				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Serse, HWV 40 (Handel, George Frideric)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1737&#8211;38 (26 December to 14 February)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<dl><dd>Gaetano Majorano, called "Caffarelli" (Serse)<br />Maria Antonia Marchesini, called "La Lucchesina" (Arsamene)<br />Antonia Maria Merighi (Amastre)<br />Elisabeth Duparc, called "La Francesina" (Romilda)<br />Margherita Chimenti, called "La Droghierina" (Atalanta)<br />Antonio Montagnana (Ariodate)<br />Antonio Lottini (Elviro) </div>
</dd></dl>
